Trace the execution of task_1 with inputs initialEnergy = task_1_initialEnergy_static, initialExperience = task_1_initialExperience_static, experience = task_1_experience_static and save the result in task_1_out.
```python
def task_1(initialEnergy: int, initialExperience: int, list_1: List[int], experience: List[int]) -> int:
    sum_energy = sum(list_1)
    energy_hours = max(0, sum_energy + 1 - initialEnergy)
    exp_hours = 0
    current_exp = initialExperience
    for e in experience:
        if current_exp <= e:
            delta = e + 1 - current_exp
            exp_hours += delta
            current_exp += delta
        current_exp += e
    task_1_out = energy_hours + exp_hours
    return task_1_out
```

Task 2:
Let val_2 be the result of preprocessing task_1_out as follows - if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_2(val_2: int, y: int, bound: int) -> List[int]:
    ans = []
    a = 1
    while a <= bound:
        b = 1
        while a + b <= bound:
            ans.append(a + b)
            b *= y
            if y == 1:
                break
        if val_2 == 1:
            break
        a *= val_2
    task_2_out = list(ans)
    return task_2_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    stk = []
    for x in list_3:
        if x > 0:
            stk.append(x)
        else:
            while stk and stk[-1] > 0 and (stk[-1] < -x):
                stk.pop()
            if stk and stk[-1] == -x:
                stk.pop()
            elif not stk or stk[-1] < 0:
                stk.append(x)
    task_3_out = stk
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    list_4.sort()
    n = len(list_4)
    f = [1] * n
    k = 0
    for i in range(n):
        for j in range(i):
            if list_4[i] % list_4[j] == 0:
                f[i] = max(f[i], f[j] + 1)
        if f[k] < f[i]:
            k = i
    m = f[k]
    i = k
    ans = []
    while m:
        if list_4[k] % list_4[i] == 0 and f[i] == m:
            ans.append(list_4[i])
            (k, m) = (i, m - 1)
        i -= 1
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

task_1_limit_static = 10
task_2_arr2_static = [-92, 77, 98, -78, -57, -15, 44, -83, 74, 41]

Task 1:
Let list_1 be the result of preprocessing task_1_input as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_1 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_1 with inputs limit = task_1_limit_static and save the result in task_1_out.
```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int], limit: int) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_1)
    arr = sorted(zip(list_1, range(n)))
    ans = [0] * n
    i = 0
    while i < n:
        j = i + 1
        while j < n and arr[j][0] - arr[j - 1][0] <= limit:
            j += 1
        idx = sorted((k for (_, k) in arr[i:j]))
        for (k, (x, _)) in zip(idx, arr[i:j]):
            ans[k] = x
        i = j
    task_1_out = ans
    return task_1_out
```

Task 2:
Let list_2 be the result of preprocessing task_1_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_2 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_2 with inputs arr2 = task_2_arr2_static and save the result in task_2_out.
```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int], arr2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    (i, j) = (len(list_2) - 1, len(arr2) - 1)
    c = 0
    ans = []
    while i >= 0 or j >= 0 or c:
        a = 0 if i < 0 else list_2[i]
        b = 0 if j < 0 else arr2[j]
        x = a + b + c
        c = 0
        if x >= 2:
            x -= 2
            c -= 1
        elif x == -1:
            x = 1
            c += 1
        ans.append(x)
        (i, j) = (i - 1, j - 1)
    while len(ans) > 1 and ans[-1] == 0:
        ans.pop()
    task_2_out = ans[::-1]
    return task_2_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    ans = []
    (i, j) = (0, len(list_3) - 1)
    while i <= j:
        a = list_3[i] * list_3[i]
        b = list_3[j] * list_3[j]
        if a > b:
            ans.append(a)
            i += 1
        else:
            ans.append(b)
            j -= 1
    task_3_out = ans[::-1]
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    ans = s = 0
    pos = {}
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_4):
        s += 1 if x > 8 else -1
        if s > 0:
            ans = i + 1
        elif s - 1 in pos:
            ans = max(ans, i - pos[s - 1])
        if s not in pos:
            pos[s] = i
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

Solve all tasks below. Put every answer in its own \boxed{} block with the exact requested output name, for example \boxed{task_1_out = ...}.

task_1_input = [35, 42, -51, 39, -4, -36, 23, -9, 60, -85]
task_4_passengers_static = [-98, -72, -71, -68, -41, 3, 19, 30, 35, 87]
task_4_capacity_static = -79

Task 1:
Let list_1 be the result of preprocessing task_1_input as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_1 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_1 and save the result in task_1_out.
```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_1)
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    stk = []
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_1):
        while stk and list_1[stk[-1]] <= x:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_1[stk[-1]] <= list_1[i]:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    task_1_out = [r - l - 1 for (l, r) in zip(left, right)]
    return task_1_out
```

Task 2:
Let list_2 be the result of preprocessing task_1_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_2 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_2 and save the result in task_2_out.
```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_2)
    leftSum = [0] * n
    for i in range(1, n):
        leftSum[i] = leftSum[i - 1] + list_2[i - 1]
    total = sum(list_2)
    answer = []
    for i in range(n):
        rightSum_i = total - list_2[i] - leftSum[i]
        answer.append(abs(leftSum[i] - rightSum_i))
    task_2_out = answer
    return task_2_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_3 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_3 and save the result in task_3_out.
```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    (i, j) = (0, len(list_3) - 1)
    while i < j:
        if list_3[i] % 2 == 0:
            i += 1
        elif list_3[j] % 2 == 1:
            j -= 1
        else:
            (list_3[i], list_3[j]) = (list_3[j], list_3[i])
            (i, j) = (i + 1, j - 1)
    task_3_out = list_3
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 with inputs passengers = task_4_passengers_static, capacity = task_4_capacity_static and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int], passengers: List[int], capacity: int) -> int:
    list_4.sort()
    passengers.sort()
    j = 0
    for t in list_4:
        c = capacity
        while c and j < len(passengers) and (passengers[j] <= t):
            (c, j) = (c - 1, j + 1)
    j -= 1
    ans = list_4[-1] if c else passengers[j]
    while ~j and passengers[j] == ans:
        (ans, j) = (ans - 1, j - 1)
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    (left, right) = (0, len(list_4) - 1)
    while left < right:
        mid = left + right >> 1
        if list_4[mid] > list_4[right]:
            left = mid + 1
        elif list_4[mid] < list_4[right]:
            right = mid
        else:
            right -= 1
    task_4_out = list_4[left]
    return task_4_out
```

Task 1:
Let list_1 be the result of preprocessing task_1_input as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_1)
    ans = [0] * n
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and stk[-1] < list_1[i]:
            ans[i] += 1
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            ans[i] += 1
        stk.append(list_1[i])
    task_1_out = ans
    return task_1_out
```

```python
        while stk and list_2[stk[-1]] <= x:
            stk.pop()

            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_2[stk[-1]] <= list_2[i]:
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    (i, j) = (0, len(list_4) - 1)
    (a, b) = (list_4[i], list_4[j])
    ans = 0
    while i < j:
        if a < b:
            i += 1
            a += list_4[i]
            ans += 1
        elif b < a:
            j -= 1
            b += list_4[j]
            ans += 1
        else:
            (i, j) = (i + 1, j - 1)
            (a, b) = (list_4[i], list_4[j])
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_1)
    leftSum = [0] * n
    for i in range(1, n):
        leftSum[i] = leftSum[i - 1] + list_1[i - 1]
    total = sum(list_1)
    answer = []
    for i in range(n):
        rightSum_i = total - list_1[i] - leftSum[i]
        answer.append(abs(leftSum[i] - rightSum_i))
    task_1_out = answer
    return task_1_out
```

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int], queries: List[int]) -> int:
    n = len(list_4)
    f = [[0] * n for _ in range(n)]
    m = len(queries)
    for i in range(n):
        for j in range(n - 1, i - 1, -1):
            if i:
                f[i][j] = max(f[i][j], f[i - 1][j] + (list_4[i - 1] >= queries[f[i - 1][j]]))
            if j + 1 < n:
                f[i][j] = max(f[i][j], f[i][j + 1] + (list_4[j + 1] >= queries[f[i][j + 1]]))
            if f[i][j] == m:
                task_4_out = m
                return task_4_out
    task_4_out = max((f[i][i] + (list_4[i] >= queries[f[i][i]]) for i in range(n)))
    return task_4_out
```

Let list_1 be the result of preprocessing task_1_input as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    stk = []
    n = len(list_1)
    ans = [0] * n
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_1[stk[-1]] <= list_1[i]:

    task_1_out = ans
```

Task 2:
Let list_2 be the result of preprocessing task_1_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:

    def reverse(arr, j):
        i = 0
        while i < j:
            (arr[i], arr[j]) = (arr[j], arr[i])
            (i, j) = (i + 1, j - 1)
    n = len(list_2)
    ans = []
    for i in range(n - 1, 0, -1):
        j = i
        while j > 0 and list_2[j] != i + 1:
            j -= 1
        if j < i:
            if j > 0:
                ans.append(j + 1)
                reverse(list_2, j)
            ans.append(i + 1)
            reverse(list_2, i)
    task_2_out = ans
    return task_2_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    stk = []
    for x in list_3:
        if x > 0:
            stk.append(x)
        else:
            while stk and stk[-1] > 0 and (stk[-1] < -x):
                stk.pop()
            if stk and stk[-1] == -x:
                stk.pop()
            elif not stk or stk[-1] < 0:
                stk.append(x)
    task_3_out = stk
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 with inputs limit = task_4_limit_static and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int], limit: int) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_4)
    arr = sorted(zip(list_4, range(n)))
    ans = [0] * n
    i = 0
    while i < n:
        j = i + 1
        while j < n and arr[j][0] - arr[j - 1][0] <= limit:
            j += 1
        idx = sorted((k for (_, k) in arr[i:j]))
        for (k, (x, _)) in zip(idx, arr[i:j]):
            ans[k] = x
        i = j
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

Task 1:
Let list_1 be the result of preprocessing task_1_input as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_1)
    ans = [-1] * n
    stk = []
    for i in range(n * 2 - 1, -1, -1):
        i %= n
        while stk and stk[-1] <= list_1[i]:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            ans[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(list_1[i])
    task_1_out = ans
    return task_1_out
```

Task 2:
Let list_2 be the result of preprocessing task_1_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_2 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_2 and save the result in task_2_out.
```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_2)
    leftSum = [0] * n
    for i in range(1, n):
        leftSum[i] = leftSum[i - 1] + list_2[i - 1]
    total = sum(list_2)
    answer = []
    for i in range(n):
        rightSum_i = total - list_2[i] - leftSum[i]
        answer.append(abs(leftSum[i] - rightSum_i))
    task_2_out = answer
    return task_2_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_3 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_3 with inputs arr2 = task_3_arr2_static and save the result in task_3_out.
```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int], arr2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    (i, j) = (len(list_3) - 1, len(arr2) - 1)
    c = 0
    ans = []
    while i >= 0 or j >= 0 or c:
        a = 0 if i < 0 else list_3[i]
        b = 0 if j < 0 else arr2[j]
        x = a + b + c
        c = 0
        if x >= 2:
            x -= 2
            c -= 1
        elif x == -1:
            x = 1
            c += 1
        ans.append(x)
        (i, j) = (i - 1, j - 1)
    while len(ans) > 1 and ans[-1] == 0:
        ans.pop()
    task_3_out = ans[::-1]
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    stk = []
    ans = 0
    for x in list_4:
        while stk and stk[-1][0] < x:
            stk.pop()
        if not stk or stk[-1][0] > x:
            stk.append([x, 1])
        else:
            stk[-1][1] += 1
        ans += stk[-1][1]
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

Task 1:
Let list_1 be the result of preprocessing task_1_input as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    (i, j) = (0, len(list_1) - 1)
    while i < j:
        if list_1[i] % 2 == 0:
            i += 1
        elif list_1[j] % 2 == 1:
            j -= 1
        else:
            (list_1[i], list_1[j]) = (list_1[j], list_1[i])
            (i, j) = (i + 1, j - 1)
    task_1_out = list_1
    return task_1_out
```

Task 2:
Let list_2 be the result of preprocessing task_1_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_2 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_2 and save the result in task_2_out.
```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_2)
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    stk = []
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_2):
        while stk and list_2[stk[-1]] <= x:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_2[stk[-1]] <= list_2[i]:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    task_2_out = [r - l - 1 for (l, r) in zip(left, right)]
    return task_2_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    ans = [0, 0]
    n = len(list_4)
    for i in range(2):
        for j in range(i, n, 2):
            d = 0
            if j:
                d = max(d, list_4[j] - list_4[j - 1] + 1)
            if j < n - 1:
                d = max(d, list_4[j] - list_4[j + 1] + 1)
            ans[i] += d
    task_4_out = min(ans)
    return task_4_out
```

Solve all tasks below. Put every answer in its own \boxed{} block with the exact requested output name, for example \boxed{task_1_out = ...}.

Task 1:
Let list_1 be the result of preprocessing task_1_input as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_1 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_1 and save the result in task_1_out.
```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    ans = []
    (i, j) = (0, len(list_1) - 1)
    while i <= j:
        a = list_1[i] * list_1[i]
        b = list_1[j] * list_1[j]
        if a > b:
            ans.append(a)
            i += 1
        else:
            ans.append(b)
            j -= 1
    task_1_out = ans[::-1]
    return task_1_out
```

Task 2:
Let list_2 be the result of preprocessing task_1_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:

    def reverse(arr, j):
        i = 0
        while i < j:
            (arr[i], arr[j]) = (arr[j], arr[i])
            (i, j) = (i + 1, j - 1)
    n = len(list_2)
    ans = []
    for i in range(n - 1, 0, -1):
        j = i
        while j > 0 and list_2[j] != i + 1:
            j -= 1
        if j < i:
            if j > 0:
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_3 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_3 and save the result in task_3_out.
```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_3)
    suf = [0] * (n + 1)
    s = set()
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        s.add(list_3[i])
        suf[i] = len(s)
    s.clear()
    ans = [0] * n
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_3):
        s.add(x)
        ans[i] = len(s) - suf[i + 1]
    task_3_out = ans
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_4)
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    stk = []
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_4):
        while stk and list_4[stk[-1]] >= x:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_4[stk[-1]] >= list_4[i]:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    ans = [0] * n
    for i in range(n):
        m = right[i] - left[i] - 1
        ans[m - 1] = max(ans[m - 1], list_4[i])
    for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
        ans[i] = max(ans[i], ans[i + 1])
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:

    for i in range(1, len(list_4) - 1):
        if list_4[i] == list_4[i + 1]:
            continue
        if list_4[i] > list_4[j] and list_4[i] > list_4[i + 1]:

        if list_4[i] < list_4[j] and list_4[i] < list_4[i + 1]:

    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int], arr2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    (i, j) = (len(list_3) - 1, len(arr2) - 1)
    c = 0
    ans = []
    while i >= 0 or j >= 0 or c:
        a = 0 if i < 0 else list_3[i]
        b = 0 if j < 0 else arr2[j]
        x = a + b + c
        c = 0
        if x >= 2:
            x -= 2
            c -= 1
        elif x == -1:
            x = 1
            c += 1
        ans.append(x)
        (i, j) = (i - 1, j - 1)

        ans.pop()
    task_3_out = ans[::-1]
    return task_3_out
```

Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int], nums2: List[int]) -> int:
    (s1, s2) = (sum(list_4), sum(nums2))
    if s1 == s2:
        task_4_out = 0
        return task_4_out
    if s1 > s2:
        task_4_out = task_4(nums2, list_4)
        return task_4_out
    arr = [6 - v for v in list_4] + [v - 1 for v in nums2]
    d = s2 - s1
    for (i, v) in enumerate(sorted(arr, reverse=True), 1):
        d -= v
        if d <= 0:
            task_4_out = i
            return task_4_out
    task_4_out = -1
    return task_4_out
```

Let list_1 be the result of preprocessing task_1_input as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

Trace the execution of task_1 and save the result in task_1_out.
```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    f = True
    while f:
        f = False
        t = list_1[:]
        for i in range(1, len(t) - 1):
            if t[i] > t[i - 1] and t[i] > t[i + 1]:
                list_1[i] -= 1
                f = True
            if t[i] < t[i - 1] and t[i] < t[i + 1]:
                list_1[i] += 1
                f = True
    task_1_out = list_1
    return task_1_out
```

Task 2:
Let list_2 be the result of preprocessing task_1_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_2)
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    stk = []
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_2):
        while stk and list_2[stk[-1]] >= x:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_2[stk[-1]] >= list_2[i]:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    ans = [0] * n
    for i in range(n):
        m = right[i] - left[i] - 1
        ans[m - 1] = max(ans[m - 1], list_2[i])
    for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
        ans[i] = max(ans[i], ans[i + 1])
    task_2_out = ans
    return task_2_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_3)
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    stk = []
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_3):
        while stk and list_3[stk[-1]] <= x:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_3[stk[-1]] <= list_3[i]:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    task_3_out = [r - l - 1 for (l, r) in zip(left, right)]
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    n = len(list_4)
    ans = 0
    for k in range(1, n + 1):
        t = 0
        j = 1
        while k * j * j <= n:
            t += list_4[k * j * j - 1]
            j += 1
        ans = max(ans, t)
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

```python
    list_1.sort()
    n = len(list_1)
    f = [1] * n
    k = 0
    for i in range(n):
        for j in range(i):
            if list_1[i] % list_1[j] == 0:
                f[i] = max(f[i], f[j] + 1)
        if f[k] < f[i]:
            k = i
    m = f[k]
```

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int], limit: int) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_3)
    arr = sorted(zip(list_3, range(n)))
    ans = [0] * n
    i = 0
    while i < n:
        j = i + 1
        while j < n and arr[j][0] - arr[j - 1][0] <= limit:
            j += 1
        idx = sorted((k for (_, k) in arr[i:j]))

            ans[k] = x
        i = j
    task_3_out = ans
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    n = len(list_4)
    left = [1] * n
    right = [1] * n
    for i in range(1, n):
        if list_4[i] > list_4[i - 1]:
            left[i] = left[i - 1] + 1
    for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
        if list_4[i] > list_4[i + 1]:
            right[i] = right[i + 1] + 1
    task_4_out = sum((max(a, b) for (a, b) in zip(left, right)))
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> int:
    n = len(list_2)
    left = [0] * (n + 1)
    right = [0] * (n + 1)
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_2, 1):
        if x:
            left[i] = left[i - 1] + 1
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        if list_2[i]:
            right[i] = right[i + 1] + 1
    task_2_out = max((left[i] + right[i + 1] for i in range(n)))
    return task_2_out
```

```python
    ans = []
    a = 1
    while a <= bound:
        b = 1
        while a + b <= bound:
            ans.append(a + b)
            b *= y
            if y == 1:
                break
        if val_3 == 1:
            break
        a *= val_3
    task_3_out = list(ans)
    return task_3_out
```

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    stk = []
    for x in list_4:
        if x > 0:
            stk.append(x)
        else:
            while stk and stk[-1] > 0 and (stk[-1] < -x):
                stk.pop()
            if stk and stk[-1] == -x:
                stk.pop()
            elif not stk or stk[-1] < 0:
                stk.append(x)
    task_4_out = stk
    return task_4_out
```

```python
    s = set()
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        s.add(list_1[i])
        suf[i] = len(s)
    s.clear()
    ans = [0] * n
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_1):
        s.add(x)
        ans[i] = len(s) - suf[i + 1]
    task_1_out = ans
    return task_1_out
```

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int], arr2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    (i, j) = (len(list_2) - 1, len(arr2) - 1)
    c = 0
    ans = []
    while i >= 0 or j >= 0 or c:
        a = 0 if i < 0 else list_2[i]
        b = 0 if j < 0 else arr2[j]
        x = a + b + c
        c = 0
        if x >= 2:
            x -= 2
            c -= 1
        elif x == -1:
            x = 1
            c += 1
        ans.append(x)
        (i, j) = (i - 1, j - 1)
    while len(ans) > 1 and ans[-1] == 0:
        ans.pop()
    task_2_out = ans[::-1]
    return task_2_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    stk = []
    for x in list_3:
        if x > 0:
            stk.append(x)
        else:
            while stk and stk[-1] > 0 and (stk[-1] < -x):
                stk.pop()
            if stk and stk[-1] == -x:
                stk.pop()
            elif not stk or stk[-1] < 0:
                stk.append(x)
    task_3_out = stk
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    n = len(list_4)
    left = [0] * (n + 1)
    right = [0] * (n + 1)
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_4, 1):
        if x:
            left[i] = left[i - 1] + 1
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        if list_4[i]:
            right[i] = right[i + 1] + 1
    task_4_out = max((left[i] + right[i + 1] for i in range(n)))
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_2)
    leftSum = [0] * n
    for i in range(1, n):
        leftSum[i] = leftSum[i - 1] + list_2[i - 1]
    total = sum(list_2)
    answer = []
    for i in range(n):
        rightSum_i = total - list_2[i] - leftSum[i]
        answer.append(abs(leftSum[i] - rightSum_i))
    task_2_out = answer
    return task_2_out
```

```python
            j += 1

        i = j
    task_3_out = ans
    return task_3_out
```

```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    ans = []
    (i, j) = (0, len(list_1) - 1)
    while i <= j:
        a = list_1[i] * list_1[i]
        b = list_1[j] * list_1[j]
        if a > b:
            ans.append(a)
            i += 1
        else:
            ans.append(b)
            j -= 1
    task_1_out = ans[::-1]
    return task_1_out
```

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_2)
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    stk = []
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_2):
        while stk and list_2[stk[-1]] <= x:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_2[stk[-1]] <= list_2[i]:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    task_2_out = [r - l - 1 for (l, r) in zip(left, right)]
```
```python
    return task_2_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_3 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_3 and save the result in task_3_out.
```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> int:
    n = len(list_3)
    f = [1] * n
    cnt = [1] * n
    mx = 0
    for i in range(n):
        for j in range(i):
            if list_3[j] < list_3[i]:
                if f[i] < f[j] + 1:
                    f[i] = f[j] + 1
                    cnt[i] = cnt[j]
                elif f[i] == f[j] + 1:
                    cnt[i] += cnt[j]
        if mx < f[i]:
            mx = f[i]
            ans = cnt[i]
        elif mx == f[i]:
            ans += cnt[i]
    task_3_out = ans
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let val_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_4(val_4: int) -> int:
    s = list(str(val_4))
    i = 1
    while i < len(s) and s[i - 1] <= s[i]:
        i += 1
    if i < len(s):
        while i and s[i - 1] > s[i]:
            s[i - 1] = str(int(s[i - 1]) - 1)
            i -= 1
        i += 1
        while i < len(s):
            s[i] = '9'
            i += 1
    task_4_out = int(''.join(s))
    return task_4_out
```

Trace the execution of task_1 with inputs y = task_1_y_static, bound = task_1_bound_static and save the result in task_1_out.
```python
def task_1(val_1: int, y: int, bound: int) -> List[int]:
    ans = []
    a = 1
    while a <= bound:
        b = 1
        while a + b <= bound:
            ans.append(a + b)
            b *= y
            if y == 1:
                break
        if val_1 == 1:
            break
        a *= val_1
    task_1_out = list(ans)
    return task_1_out
```

Task 2:
Let list_2 be the result of preprocessing task_1_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_2)
    ans = [0] * n
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and stk[-1] < list_2[i]:
            ans[i] += 1
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            ans[i] += 1
        stk.append(list_2[i])
    task_2_out = ans
    return task_2_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_3 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_3 and save the result in task_3_out.
```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_3)
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    stk = []
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_3):
        while stk and list_3[stk[-1]] >= x:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_3[stk[-1]] >= list_3[i]:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    ans = [0] * n
    for i in range(n):
        m = right[i] - left[i] - 1
        ans[m - 1] = max(ans[m - 1], list_3[i])
    for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
        ans[i] = max(ans[i], ans[i + 1])
    task_3_out = ans
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    n = len(list_4)
    ans = 1
    f = [1] * n
    g = [1] * n
    for i in range(1, n):
        for j in range(i):
            if list_4[j] < list_4[i]:
                f[i] = max(f[i], g[j] + 1)
            elif list_4[j] > list_4[i]:
                g[i] = max(g[i], f[j] + 1)
        ans = max(ans, f[i], g[i])
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

```python
    c = 0
    ans = []
    while i >= 0 or j >= 0 or c:
        a = 0 if i < 0 else list_1[i]
        b = 0 if j < 0 else arr2[j]
        x = a + b + c
        c = 0

            c -= 1
        elif x == -1:
            x = 1
            c += 1
        ans.append(x)
        (i, j) = (i - 1, j - 1)

        ans.pop()
    task_1_out = ans[::-1]
```

```python
        if x == 0:
            task_4_out = 1
            return task_4_out
        if x * y <= k:
            y *= x
        else:
            y = x
            ans += 1
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

```python
    while i < j:
        if list_1[i] % 2 == 0:
            i += 1

            j -= 1
        else:
```

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int], limit: int) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_3)
    arr = sorted(zip(list_3, range(n)))
    ans = [0] * n
    i = 0
    while i < n:
        j = i + 1
        while j < n and arr[j][0] - arr[j - 1][0] <= limit:
            j += 1
        idx = sorted((k for (_, k) in arr[i:j]))
        for (k, (x, _)) in zip(idx, arr[i:j]):
            ans[k] = x
        i = j
    task_3_out = ans
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:

    def f(x: int) -> int:
        i = 2
        (cnt, s) = (2, x + 1)
        while i <= x // i:
            if x % i == 0:
                cnt += 1
                s += i
                if i * i != x:
                    cnt += 1
                    s += x // i
            i += 1
        return s if cnt == 4 else 0
    task_4_out = sum((f(x) for x in list_4))
    return task_4_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> List[int]:

    def reverse(arr, j):
        i = 0
        while i < j:
            (arr[i], arr[j]) = (arr[j], arr[i])
            (i, j) = (i + 1, j - 1)
    n = len(list_4)
    ans = []
    for i in range(n - 1, 0, -1):
        j = i
        while j > 0 and list_4[j] != i + 1:
            j -= 1
        if j < i:
            if j > 0:
                ans.append(j + 1)
                reverse(list_4, j)
            ans.append(i + 1)
            reverse(list_4, i)
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    stk = []
    for x in list_3:
        if x > 0:
            stk.append(x)
        else:
            while stk and stk[-1] > 0 and (stk[-1] < -x):
                stk.pop()
            if stk and stk[-1] == -x:
                stk.pop()
            elif not stk or stk[-1] < 0:
                stk.append(x)
    task_3_out = stk
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    if list_4[0] <= list_4[-1]:
        task_4_out = list_4[0]
        return task_4_out
    (left, right) = (0, len(list_4) - 1)
    while left < right:
        mid = left + right >> 1
        if list_4[0] <= list_4[mid]:
            left = mid + 1
        else:
            right = mid
    task_4_out = list_4[left]
    return task_4_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_3 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_3 and save the result in task_3_out.
```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_3)
    leftSum = [0] * n
    for i in range(1, n):
        leftSum[i] = leftSum[i - 1] + list_3[i - 1]
    total = sum(list_3)
    answer = []
    for i in range(n):
        rightSum_i = total - list_3[i] - leftSum[i]
        answer.append(abs(leftSum[i] - rightSum_i))
    task_3_out = answer
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    (l, r) = (0, len(list_4) - 1)
    ans = 0
    while l < r:
        t = min(list_4[l], list_4[r]) * (r - l)
        ans = max(ans, t)
        if list_4[l] < list_4[r]:
            l += 1
        else:
            r -= 1
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_1)
    leftSum = [0] * n
    for i in range(1, n):
        leftSum[i] = leftSum[i - 1] + list_1[i - 1]
    total = sum(list_1)
    answer = []
    for i in range(n):
        rightSum_i = total - list_1[i] - leftSum[i]
        answer.append(abs(leftSum[i] - rightSum_i))
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int], arr2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    (i, j) = (len(list_3) - 1, len(arr2) - 1)
    c = 0
    ans = []
    while i >= 0 or j >= 0 or c:
        a = 0 if i < 0 else list_3[i]
        b = 0 if j < 0 else arr2[j]
        x = a + b + c
        c = 0
        if x >= 2:
            x -= 2
            c -= 1
        elif x == -1:
            x = 1
            c += 1
        ans.append(x)
        (i, j) = (i - 1, j - 1)
    while len(ans) > 1 and ans[-1] == 0:
        ans.pop()
    task_3_out = ans[::-1]
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    n = len(list_4)
    left = [0] * n
    right = [0] * n
    s = 0
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_4):
        s = max(s, 0) + x
        left[i] = s
    s = 0
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        s = max(s, 0) + list_4[i]
        right[i] = s
    ans = max(left)
    for i in range(1, n - 1):
        ans = max(ans, left[i - 1] + right[i + 1])
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_3)
    suf = [0] * (n + 1)
    s = set()
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        s.add(list_3[i])
        suf[i] = len(s)
    s.clear()
    ans = [0] * n
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_3):
        s.add(x)
        ans[i] = len(s) - suf[i + 1]
    task_3_out = ans
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    n = len(list_4)
    stk = []
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    for (i, h) in enumerate(list_4):
        while stk and list_4[stk[-1]] >= h:
            right[stk[-1]] = i
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    task_4_out = max((h * (right[i] - left[i] - 1) for (i, h) in enumerate(list_4)))
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_1)
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    stk = []
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_1):
        while stk and list_1[stk[-1]] <= x:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_1[stk[-1]] <= list_1[i]:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    task_1_out = [r - l - 1 for (l, r) in zip(left, right)]
    return task_1_out
```

```python
        if list_4[i] < list_4[j]:
            i = j
            cnt = 1
        else:
            cnt += 1
        if cnt == k:
            break
    task_4_out = i
    return task_4_out
```

Task 2:
Let list_2 be the result of preprocessing task_1_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_2 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_2 and save the result in task_2_out.
```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_2)
    leftSum = [0] * n
    for i in range(1, n):
        leftSum[i] = leftSum[i - 1] + list_2[i - 1]
    total = sum(list_2)
    answer = []
    for i in range(n):
        rightSum_i = total - list_2[i] - leftSum[i]
        answer.append(abs(leftSum[i] - rightSum_i))
    task_2_out = answer
    return task_2_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_3 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_3 with inputs limit = task_3_limit_static and save the result in task_3_out.
```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int], limit: int) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_3)
    arr = sorted(zip(list_3, range(n)))
    ans = [0] * n
    i = 0
    while i < n:
        j = i + 1
        while j < n and arr[j][0] - arr[j - 1][0] <= limit:
            j += 1
        idx = sorted((k for (_, k) in arr[i:j]))
        for (k, (x, _)) in zip(idx, arr[i:j]):
            ans[k] = x
        i = j
    task_3_out = ans
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 with inputs k = task_4_k_static and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int], k: int) -> int:
    s = mx_pre = mi_pre = mx_sub = 0
    for x in list_4:
        s += x
        mx_pre = max(mx_pre, s)
        mi_pre = min(mi_pre, s)
        mx_sub = max(mx_sub, s - mi_pre)
    ans = mx_sub
    mod = 10 ** 9 + 7
    if k == 1:
        task_4_out = ans % mod
        return task_4_out
    mx_suf = s - mi_pre
    ans = max(ans, mx_pre + mx_suf)
    if s > 0:
        ans = max(ans, (k - 2) * s + mx_pre + mx_suf)
    task_4_out = ans % mod
    return task_4_out
```

Task 2:
Let list_2 be the result of preprocessing task_1_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    ans = []
    (i, j) = (0, len(list_2) - 1)
    while i <= j:
        a = list_2[i] * list_2[i]
        b = list_2[j] * list_2[j]
        if a > b:
            ans.append(a)
            i += 1
        else:
            ans.append(b)
            j -= 1
    task_2_out = ans[::-1]
    return task_2_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_3 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_3 with inputs arr2 = task_3_arr2_static and save the result in task_3_out.
```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int], arr2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    (i, j) = (len(list_3) - 1, len(arr2) - 1)
    c = 0
    ans = []
    while i >= 0 or j >= 0 or c:
        a = 0 if i < 0 else list_3[i]
        b = 0 if j < 0 else arr2[j]
        x = a + b + c
        c = 0
        if x >= 2:
            x -= 2
            c -= 1
        elif x == -1:
            x = 1
            c += 1
        ans.append(x)
        (i, j) = (i - 1, j - 1)
    while len(ans) > 1 and ans[-1] == 0:
        ans.pop()
    task_3_out = ans[::-1]
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int], capacityA: int, capacityB: int) -> int:
    (a, b) = (capacityA, capacityB)
    ans = 0
    (i, j) = (0, len(list_4) - 1)
    while i < j:
        if a < list_4[i]:
            ans += 1
            a = capacityA
        a -= list_4[i]
        if b < list_4[j]:
            ans += 1
            b = capacityB
        b -= list_4[j]
        (i, j) = (i + 1, j - 1)
    ans += i == j and max(a, b) < list_4[i]
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_3)
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    stk = []
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_3):
        while stk and list_3[stk[-1]] >= x:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_3[stk[-1]] >= list_3[i]:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    ans = [0] * n
    for i in range(n):
        m = right[i] - left[i] - 1
        ans[m - 1] = max(ans[m - 1], list_3[i])
    for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
        ans[i] = max(ans[i], ans[i + 1])
    task_3_out = ans
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

Trace the execution of task_4 with inputs nums2 = task_4_nums2_static and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int], nums2: List[int]) -> int:
    nums = [a - b for (a, b) in zip(list_4, nums2)]
    nums.sort()
    (l, r) = (0, len(nums) - 1)
    ans = 0
    while l < r:
        while l < r and nums[l] + nums[r] <= 0:
            l += 1
        ans += r - l
        r -= 1
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    list_1.sort()
    n = len(list_1)
    f = [1] * n
    k = 0
    for i in range(n):
        for j in range(i):
            if list_1[i] % list_1[j] == 0:
                f[i] = max(f[i], f[j] + 1)
        if f[k] < f[i]:
            k = i
    m = f[k]
    i = k
    ans = []
    while m:
        if list_1[k] % list_1[i] == 0 and f[i] == m:
            ans.append(list_1[i])
            (k, m) = (i, m - 1)
        i -= 1
    task_1_out = ans
    return task_1_out
```

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_2)
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    stk = []
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_2):
        while stk and list_2[stk[-1]] <= x:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_2[stk[-1]] <= list_2[i]:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    task_2_out = [r - l - 1 for (l, r) in zip(left, right)]
    return task_2_out
```

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    (i, j) = (0, len(list_3) - 1)
    while i < j:
        if list_3[i] % 2 == 0:
            i += 1
        elif list_3[j] % 2 == 1:
            j -= 1
        else:
            (list_3[i], list_3[j]) = (list_3[j], list_3[i])
            (i, j) = (i + 1, j - 1)
    task_3_out = list_3
    return task_3_out
```

```python
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
```

```python
    ans = [0] * n
    i = 0

        while j < n and arr[j][0] - arr[j - 1][0] <= limit:
            j += 1
```

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    stk = []
    for x in list_2:
        if x > 0:
            stk.append(x)
        else:
            while stk and stk[-1] > 0 and (stk[-1] < -x):
                stk.pop()
            if stk and stk[-1] == -x:
                stk.pop()
            elif not stk or stk[-1] < 0:
                stk.append(x)

    return task_2_out
```

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_3)
    suf = [0] * (n + 1)
    s = set()
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        s.add(list_3[i])
        suf[i] = len(s)
    s.clear()
    ans = [0] * n
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_3):
        s.add(x)
        ans[i] = len(s) - suf[i + 1]
    task_3_out = ans
    return task_3_out
```

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int], target: int) -> int:
    list_4.sort()
    (ans, n) = (0, len(list_4))
    for i in range(n - 2):
        (j, k) = (i + 1, n - 1)
        while j < k:
            x = list_4[i] + list_4[j] + list_4[k]
            if x < target:
                ans += k - j
                j += 1
            else:
                k -= 1
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

```python
        b = 0 if j < 0 else arr2[j]
        x = a + b + c
```

Task 1:
Let list_1 be the result of preprocessing task_1_input as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_1 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_1 and save the result in task_1_out.
```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:

    def reverse(arr, j):
        i = 0
        while i < j:
            (arr[i], arr[j]) = (arr[j], arr[i])
            (i, j) = (i + 1, j - 1)
    n = len(list_1)
    ans = []
    for i in range(n - 1, 0, -1):
        j = i
        while j > 0 and list_1[j] != i + 1:
            j -= 1
        if j < i:
            if j > 0:
                ans.append(j + 1)
                reverse(list_1, j)
            ans.append(i + 1)
            reverse(list_1, i)
    task_1_out = ans
    return task_1_out
```

Task 2:
Let list_2 be the result of preprocessing task_1_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
    while i <= j:
        a = list_2[i] * list_2[i]
        b = list_2[j] * list_2[j]
        if a > b:
            ans.append(a)
            i += 1
        else:
            ans.append(b)
            j -= 1
    task_2_out = ans[::-1]
    return task_2_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int], nums2: List[int]) -> int:
    mod = 10 ** 9 + 7
    (m, n) = (len(list_4), len(nums2))
    i = j = 0
    f = g = 0
    while i < m or j < n:
        if i == m:
            g += nums2[j]
            j += 1
        elif j == n:
            f += list_4[i]
            i += 1
        elif list_4[i] < nums2[j]:
            f += list_4[i]
            i += 1
        elif list_4[i] > nums2[j]:
            g += nums2[j]
            j += 1
        else:
            f = g = max(f, g) + list_4[i]
            i += 1
            j += 1
    task_4_out = max(f, g) % mod
    return task_4_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

Trace the execution of task_3 and save the result in task_3_out.
```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    f = True
    while f:
        f = False
        t = list_3[:]
        for i in range(1, len(t) - 1):
            if t[i] > t[i - 1] and t[i] > t[i + 1]:
                list_3[i] -= 1
                f = True
            if t[i] < t[i - 1] and t[i] < t[i + 1]:
                list_3[i] += 1
                f = True
    task_3_out = list_3
    return task_3_out
```

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_2)
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    stk = []
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_2):
        while stk and list_2[stk[-1]] <= x:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_2[stk[-1]] <= list_2[i]:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:

        stk.append(i)
```

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_3)
    leftSum = [0] * n
    for i in range(1, n):
        leftSum[i] = leftSum[i - 1] + list_3[i - 1]
    total = sum(list_3)
    answer = []
    for i in range(n):
        rightSum_i = total - list_3[i] - leftSum[i]
        answer.append(abs(leftSum[i] - rightSum_i))
    task_3_out = answer
    return task_3_out
```

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:

    def reverse(arr, j):
        i = 0
        while i < j:
            (arr[i], arr[j]) = (arr[j], arr[i])
            (i, j) = (i + 1, j - 1)
    n = len(list_3)
    ans = []
    for i in range(n - 1, 0, -1):
        j = i
        while j > 0 and list_3[j] != i + 1:
            j -= 1
        if j < i:
            if j > 0:
                ans.append(j + 1)
                reverse(list_3, j)
            ans.append(i + 1)
            reverse(list_3, i)
    task_3_out = ans
    return task_3_out
```

```python
            j -= 1
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    list_3.sort()
    n = len(list_3)
    f = [1] * n
    k = 0
    for i in range(n):
        for j in range(i):
            if list_3[i] % list_3[j] == 0:
                f[i] = max(f[i], f[j] + 1)
        if f[k] < f[i]:
            k = i
    m = f[k]
    i = k
    ans = []
    while m:
        if list_3[k] % list_3[i] == 0 and f[i] == m:
            ans.append(list_3[i])
            (k, m) = (i, m - 1)
        i -= 1
    task_3_out = ans
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    (i, n) = (0, len(list_4))
    while i + 1 < n and list_4[i] < list_4[i + 1]:
        i += 1
    if i == n - 1:
        task_4_out = n * (n + 1) // 2
        return task_4_out
    ans = i + 2
    j = n - 1
    while j:
        while i >= 0 and list_4[i] >= list_4[j]:
            i -= 1
        ans += i + 2
        if list_4[j - 1] >= list_4[j]:
            break
        j -= 1
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_2(initialEnergy: int, initialExperience: int, list_2: List[int], experience: List[int]) -> int:
    sum_energy = sum(list_2)
    energy_hours = max(0, sum_energy + 1 - initialEnergy)
    exp_hours = 0
    current_exp = initialExperience
    for e in experience:
        if current_exp <= e:
            delta = e + 1 - current_exp
            exp_hours += delta
            current_exp += delta
        current_exp += e
    task_2_out = energy_hours + exp_hours
    return task_2_out
```

```python
        (t, s, i) = (val_3, 0, 2)

            while val_3 % i == 0:
                val_3 //= i
                s += i
            i += 1

        val_3 = s
```

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    stk = []
    for x in list_2:
        if x > 0:
            stk.append(x)
        else:
            while stk and stk[-1] > 0 and (stk[-1] < -x):
                stk.pop()
            if stk and stk[-1] == -x:
                stk.pop()
            elif not stk or stk[-1] < 0:
                stk.append(x)
    task_2_out = stk
    return task_2_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    n = len(list_4)
    f = [[0] * n for _ in range(n)]
    d = {x: i for (i, x) in enumerate(list_4)}
    for i in range(n):
        for j in range(i):
            f[i][j] = 2
    ans = 0
    for i in range(2, n):
        for j in range(1, i):
            t = list_4[i] - list_4[j]
            if t in d and (k := d[t]) < j:
                f[i][j] = max(f[i][j], f[j][k] + 1)
                ans = max(ans, f[i][j])
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_1)
    suf = [0] * (n + 1)
    s = set()
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        s.add(list_1[i])
        suf[i] = len(s)
    s.clear()
    ans = [0] * n
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_1):
        s.add(x)
        ans[i] = len(s) - suf[i + 1]
    task_1_out = ans
    return task_1_out
```

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int], limit: int) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_2)
    arr = sorted(zip(list_2, range(n)))
    ans = [0] * n
    i = 0
    while i < n:
        j = i + 1
        while j < n and arr[j][0] - arr[j - 1][0] <= limit:
            j += 1
        idx = sorted((k for (_, k) in arr[i:j]))
        for (k, (x, _)) in zip(idx, arr[i:j]):
            ans[k] = x
        i = j
    task_2_out = ans
    return task_2_out
```

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:

    def reverse(arr, j):
        i = 0
        while i < j:
            (arr[i], arr[j]) = (arr[j], arr[i])
            (i, j) = (i + 1, j - 1)
    n = len(list_2)
    ans = []

        j = i

            reverse(list_2, i)
```

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    list_3.sort()
    n = len(list_3)
    f = [1] * n
    k = 0
    for i in range(n):
        for j in range(i):
            if list_3[i] % list_3[j] == 0:
                f[i] = max(f[i], f[j] + 1)
        if f[k] < f[i]:
            k = i
    m = f[k]
    i = k
    ans = []
    while m:
        if list_3[k] % list_3[i] == 0 and f[i] == m:
            ans.append(list_3[i])
            (k, m) = (i, m - 1)
        i -= 1
    task_3_out = ans
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    n = len(list_4)
    max_total = 0
    for i in range(n):
        left = [0] * (i + 1)
        left[i] = list_4[i]
        for j in range(i - 1, -1, -1):
            left[j] = min(list_4[j], left[j + 1])
        left_sum = sum(left)
        right_length = n - i
        right = [0] * right_length
        right[0] = list_4[i]
        for j in range(i + 1, n):
            pos_in_right = j - i
            right[pos_in_right] = min(list_4[j], right[pos_in_right - 1])
        right_sum = sum(right)
        current_total = left_sum + right_sum - list_4[i]
        if current_total > max_total:
            max_total = current_total
    task_4_out = max_total
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    n = len(list_4)
    stk = []
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    for (i, h) in enumerate(list_4):
        while stk and list_4[stk[-1]] >= h:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        h = list_4[i]
        while stk and list_4[stk[-1]] >= h:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    task_4_out = max((h * (right[i] - left[i] - 1) for (i, h) in enumerate(list_4)))
    return task_4_out
```

Task 3:

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_3)
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    stk = []
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_3):
        while stk and list_3[stk[-1]] >= x:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_3[stk[-1]] >= list_3[i]:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    ans = [0] * n
    for i in range(n):
        m = right[i] - left[i] - 1
        ans[m - 1] = max(ans[m - 1], list_3[i])
    for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
        ans[i] = max(ans[i], ans[i + 1])
    task_3_out = ans
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 with inputs k = task_4_k_static and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int], k: int) -> int:
    if list_4[0] > k:
        task_4_out = k
        return task_4_out
    (left, right) = (0, len(list_4))
    while left < right:
        mid = left + right >> 1
        if list_4[mid] - mid - 1 >= k:
            right = mid
        else:
            left = mid + 1
    task_4_out = list_4[left - 1] + k - (list_4[left - 1] - (left - 1) - 1)
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_1)
    suf = [0] * (n + 1)
    s = set()
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        s.add(list_1[i])
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_3)
    leftSum = [0] * n
    for i in range(1, n):
        leftSum[i] = leftSum[i - 1] + list_3[i - 1]
    total = sum(list_3)
    answer = []
    for i in range(n):
        rightSum_i = total - list_3[i] - leftSum[i]
        answer.append(abs(leftSum[i] - rightSum_i))
    task_3_out = answer
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    n = len(list_4)
    f = [[0] * n for _ in range(n)]
    g = [[0] * n for _ in range(n)]
    for j in range(1, n - 2):
        cnt = sum((list_4[l] > list_4[j] for l in range(j + 1, n)))
        for k in range(j + 1, n - 1):
            if list_4[j] > list_4[k]:
                f[j][k] = cnt
            else:
                cnt -= 1
    for k in range(2, n - 1):
        cnt = sum((list_4[i] < list_4[k] for i in range(k)))
        for j in range(k - 1, 0, -1):
            if list_4[j] > list_4[k]:
                g[j][k] = cnt
            else:
                cnt -= 1
    task_4_out = sum((f[j][k] * g[j][k] for j in range(1, n - 2) for k in range(j + 1, n - 1)))
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    f = True
    while f:
        f = False
        t = list_3[:]
        for i in range(1, len(t) - 1):
            if t[i] > t[i - 1] and t[i] > t[i + 1]:
                list_3[i] -= 1
                f = True
            if t[i] < t[i - 1] and t[i] < t[i + 1]:
                list_3[i] += 1
                f = True
    task_3_out = list_3
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    n = len(list_4)
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    stk = []
    for (i, v) in enumerate(list_4):
        while stk and list_4[stk[-1]] >= v:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_4[stk[-1]] > list_4[i]:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    mod = 10 ** 9 + 7
    task_4_out = sum(((i - left[i]) * (right[i] - i) * v for (i, v) in enumerate(list_4))) % mod
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_1)
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    stk = []
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_1):
        while stk and list_1[stk[-1]] <= x:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_1[stk[-1]] <= list_1[i]:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)

    return task_1_out
```

Task 2:
Let list_2 be the result of preprocessing task_1_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    list_2.sort()
    n = len(list_2)
    f = [1] * n
    k = 0
    for i in range(n):
        for j in range(i):
            if list_2[i] % list_2[j] == 0:
                f[i] = max(f[i], f[j] + 1)
        if f[k] < f[i]:
            k = i
    m = f[k]
    i = k
    ans = []
    while m:
        if list_2[k] % list_2[i] == 0 and f[i] == m:
            ans.append(list_2[i])
            (k, m) = (i, m - 1)
        i -= 1
    task_2_out = ans
    return task_2_out
```
