Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    mod = 10 ** 9 + 7
    n = len(list_4)
    list_4.sort()
    idx = {v: i for (i, v) in enumerate(list_4)}
    f = [1] * n
    for (i, a) in enumerate(list_4):
        for j in range(i):
            b = list_4[j]
            if a % b == 0 and (c := (a // b)) in idx:
                f[i] = (f[i] + f[j] * f[idx[c]]) % mod
    task_4_out = sum(f) % mod
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:

    leftSum = [0] * n

        leftSum[i] = leftSum[i - 1] + list_3[i - 1]

    answer = []

    return task_3_out
```

Task 2:
Let list_2 be the result of preprocessing task_1_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_2)
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    stk = []
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_2):
        while stk and list_2[stk[-1]] >= x:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_2[stk[-1]] >= list_2[i]:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    ans = [0] * n
    for i in range(n):
        m = right[i] - left[i] - 1
        ans[m - 1] = max(ans[m - 1], list_2[i])
    for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
        ans[i] = max(ans[i], ans[i + 1])
    task_2_out = ans
    return task_2_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int], queries: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    s = set()
    ans = []
    for q in queries[::-1]:
        if q not in s:
            ans.append(q)
            s.add(q)
    for w in list_3:
        if w not in s:
            ans.append(w)
    task_3_out = ans
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    n = len(list_4)
    stk = []
    left = [-1] * n
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_4):
        while stk and list_4[stk[-1]] > x:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    right = [n] * n
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        x = list_4[i]
        while stk and list_4[stk[-1]] >= x:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    f = [0] * n
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_4):
        if i and x >= list_4[i - 1]:
            f[i] = f[i - 1] + x
        else:
            j = left[i]
            f[i] = x * (i - j) + (f[j] if j != -1 else 0)
    g = [0] * n
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        if i < n - 1 and list_4[i] >= list_4[i + 1]:
            g[i] = g[i + 1] + list_4[i]
        else:
            j = right[i]
            g[i] = list_4[i] * (j - i) + (g[j] if j != n else 0)
    task_4_out = max((a + b - c for (a, b, c) in zip(f, g, list_4)))
    return task_4_out
```

Task 1:
Let list_1 be the result of preprocessing task_1_input as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_1 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_1 and save the result in task_1_out.
```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:

    def reverse(arr, j):
        i = 0
        while i < j:
            (arr[i], arr[j]) = (arr[j], arr[i])
            (i, j) = (i + 1, j - 1)
    n = len(list_1)
    ans = []
    for i in range(n - 1, 0, -1):
        j = i
        while j > 0 and list_1[j] != i + 1:
            j -= 1
        if j < i:
            if j > 0:
                ans.append(j + 1)
                reverse(list_1, j)
            ans.append(i + 1)
            reverse(list_1, i)
    task_1_out = ans
    return task_1_out
```

Task 2:
Let list_2 be the result of preprocessing task_1_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_2 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_2 and save the result in task_2_out.
```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_2)
    leftSum = [0] * n
    for i in range(1, n):
        leftSum[i] = leftSum[i - 1] + list_2[i - 1]
    total = sum(list_2)
    answer = []
    for i in range(n):
        rightSum_i = total - list_2[i] - leftSum[i]
        answer.append(abs(leftSum[i] - rightSum_i))
    task_2_out = answer
    return task_2_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_3 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_3)
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    stk = []
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_3):
        while stk and list_3[stk[-1]] <= x:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_3[stk[-1]] <= list_3[i]:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    task_3_out = [r - l - 1 for (l, r) in zip(left, right)]
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:

    def dfs(nums):
        if len(nums) < 2:
            return 1
        left = [x for x in nums if x < nums[0]]
        right = [x for x in nums if x > nums[0]]
        (m, n) = (len(left), len(right))
        (a, b) = (dfs(left), dfs(right))
        return c[m + n][m] * a % mod * b % mod
    n = len(list_4)
    mod = 10 ** 9 + 7
    c = [[0] * n for _ in range(n)]
    c[0][0] = 1
    for i in range(1, n):
        c[i][0] = 1
        for j in range(1, i + 1):
            c[i][j] = (c[i - 1][j] + c[i - 1][j - 1]) % mod
    task_4_out = (dfs(list_4) - 1 + mod) % mod
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int], limit: int) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_1)
    arr = sorted(zip(list_1, range(n)))
    ans = [0] * n
    i = 0
    while i < n:
        j = i + 1
        while j < n and arr[j][0] - arr[j - 1][0] <= limit:
            j += 1
        idx = sorted((k for (_, k) in arr[i:j]))
        for (k, (x, _)) in zip(idx, arr[i:j]):
            ans[k] = x
        i = j
    task_1_out = ans
    return task_1_out
```

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    f = True
    while f:
        f = False
        t = list_3[:]
        for i in range(1, len(t) - 1):
            if t[i] > t[i - 1] and t[i] > t[i + 1]:
                list_3[i] -= 1
                f = True
            if t[i] < t[i - 1] and t[i] < t[i + 1]:
                list_3[i] += 1
                f = True
    task_3_out = list_3
    return task_3_out
```

```python
            t = 1

        if list_4[i] > x:
            t += 1
            ans = max(ans, t)
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    (i, n) = (0, len(list_4))
    while i + 1 < n and list_4[i] < list_4[i + 1]:
        i += 1
    if i == n - 1:
        task_4_out = n * (n + 1) // 2
        return task_4_out
    ans = i + 2
    j = n - 1
    while j:
        while i >= 0 and list_4[i] >= list_4[j]:
            i -= 1
        ans += i + 2
        if list_4[j - 1] >= list_4[j]:
            break
        j -= 1
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

Let list_1 be the result of preprocessing task_1_input as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_1 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.

```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    ans = []
    (i, j) = (0, len(list_1) - 1)
    while i <= j:
        a = list_1[i] * list_1[i]
        b = list_1[j] * list_1[j]
        if a > b:
            ans.append(a)
            i += 1
        else:
            ans.append(b)
            j -= 1
    task_1_out = ans[::-1]
    return task_1_out
```

Task 2:
Let list_2 be the result of preprocessing task_1_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> int:
    n = len(list_2)
    f = [1] * n
    g = [1] * n
    for i in range(1, n):
        if list_2[i] > list_2[i - 1]:
            f[i] = f[i - 1] + 1
    ans = 0
    for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
        if list_2[i] > list_2[i + 1]:
            g[i] = g[i + 1] + 1
            if f[i] > 1:
                ans = max(ans, f[i] + g[i] - 1)
    task_2_out = ans
    return task_2_out
```

Task 3:
Let val_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_3(val_3: int, y: int, bound: int) -> List[int]:
    ans = []
    a = 1
    while a <= bound:
        b = 1
        while a + b <= bound:
            ans.append(a + b)
            b *= y
            if y == 1:
                break
        if val_3 == 1:
            break
        a *= val_3
    task_3_out = list(ans)
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    n = len(list_4)
    f = [1] * n
    cnt = [1] * n
    mx = 0
    for i in range(n):
        for j in range(i):
            if list_4[j] < list_4[i]:
                if f[i] < f[j] + 1:
                    f[i] = f[j] + 1
                    cnt[i] = cnt[j]
                elif f[i] == f[j] + 1:
                    cnt[i] += cnt[j]
        if mx < f[i]:
            mx = f[i]
            ans = cnt[i]
        elif mx == f[i]:
            ans += cnt[i]
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_4)
    suf = [0] * (n + 1)
    s = set()
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        s.add(list_4[i])
        suf[i] = len(s)
    s.clear()
    ans = [0] * n
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_4):
        s.add(x)
        ans[i] = len(s) - suf[i + 1]
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_3 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_3 with inputs passengers = task_3_passengers_static, capacity = task_3_capacity_static and save the result in task_3_out.
```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int], passengers: List[int], capacity: int) -> int:
    list_3.sort()
    passengers.sort()
    j = 0
    for t in list_3:
        c = capacity
        while c and j < len(passengers) and (passengers[j] <= t):
            (c, j) = (c - 1, j + 1)
    j -= 1
    ans = list_3[-1] if c else passengers[j]
    while ~j and passengers[j] == ans:
        (ans, j) = (ans - 1, j - 1)
    task_3_out = ans
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let val_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(val_4: int) -> int:
    ans = 0
    (mi, mx) = (-2 ** 31, 2 ** 31 - 1)
    while val_4:
        if ans < mi // 10 + 1 or ans > mx // 10:
            task_4_out = 0
            return task_4_out
        y = val_4 % 10
        if val_4 < 0 and y > 0:
            y -= 10
        ans = ans * 10 + y
        val_4 = (val_4 - y) // 10
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int], warehouse: List[int]) -> int:
    n = len(warehouse)
    left = [warehouse[0]] * n
    for i in range(1, n):
        left[i] = min(left[i - 1], warehouse[i])
    list_4.sort()
    (i, j) = (0, n - 1)
    while i < len(list_4):
        while j >= 0 and left[j] < list_4[i]:
            j -= 1
        if j < 0:
            break
        (i, j) = (i + 1, j - 1)
    task_4_out = i
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    ans = []
    (i, j) = (0, len(list_1) - 1)
    while i <= j:
        a = list_1[i] * list_1[i]
        b = list_1[j] * list_1[j]
        if a > b:
            ans.append(a)
            i += 1
        else:
            ans.append(b)
            j -= 1
    task_1_out = ans[::-1]
    return task_1_out
```

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:

    def reverse(arr, j):
        i = 0
        while i < j:
            (arr[i], arr[j]) = (arr[j], arr[i])
            (i, j) = (i + 1, j - 1)
    n = len(list_2)
    ans = []
    for i in range(n - 1, 0, -1):
        j = i
        while j > 0 and list_2[j] != i + 1:
            j -= 1
        if j < i:
            if j > 0:
                ans.append(j + 1)
                reverse(list_2, j)
            ans.append(i + 1)
            reverse(list_2, i)
    task_2_out = ans
    return task_2_out
```

```python
def task_4(initialEnergy: int, initialExperience: int, list_4: List[int], experience: List[int]) -> int:
    sum_energy = sum(list_4)
    energy_hours = max(0, sum_energy + 1 - initialEnergy)
    exp_hours = 0
    current_exp = initialExperience
    for e in experience:
        if current_exp <= e:
            delta = e + 1 - current_exp
            exp_hours += delta
            current_exp += delta
        current_exp += e
    task_4_out = energy_hours + exp_hours
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    g = []
    for x in list_4:
        (l, r) = (0, len(g))
        while l < r:
            mid = l + r >> 1
            if g[mid] < x:
                r = mid
            else:
                l = mid + 1
        if l == len(g):
            g.append(x)
        else:
            g[l] = x
    task_4_out = len(g)
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_2)
    leftSum = [0] * n
    for i in range(1, n):
        leftSum[i] = leftSum[i - 1] + list_2[i - 1]

    return task_2_out
```

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int], limit: int) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_2)
    arr = sorted(zip(list_2, range(n)))
    ans = [0] * n
    i = 0
    while i < n:
        j = i + 1
        while j < n and arr[j][0] - arr[j - 1][0] <= limit:
            j += 1
        idx = sorted((k for (_, k) in arr[i:j]))
        for (k, (x, _)) in zip(idx, arr[i:j]):
            ans[k] = x
        i = j
    task_2_out = ans
    return task_2_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

Trace the execution of task_4 with inputs nums2 = task_4_nums2_static and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int], nums2: List[int]) -> int:

    def f(nums1, nums2):
        d = [a - b for (a, b) in zip(nums1, nums2)]
        t = mx = d[0]
        for v in d[1:]:
            if t > 0:
                t += v
            else:
                t = v
            mx = max(mx, t)
        return mx
    (s1, s2) = (sum(list_4), sum(nums2))
    task_4_out = max(s2 + f(list_4, nums2), s1 + f(nums2, list_4))
    return task_4_out
```

```python
    leftSum = [0] * n
    for i in range(1, n):
        leftSum[i] = leftSum[i - 1] + list_2[i - 1]
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:

    def reverse(arr, j):
        i = 0
        while i < j:
            (arr[i], arr[j]) = (arr[j], arr[i])
            (i, j) = (i + 1, j - 1)
    n = len(list_3)
    ans = []
    for i in range(n - 1, 0, -1):
        j = i
        while j > 0 and list_3[j] != i + 1:
            j -= 1
        if j < i:
            if j > 0:
                ans.append(j + 1)
                reverse(list_3, j)
            ans.append(i + 1)
            reverse(list_3, i)
    task_3_out = ans
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    s = set()
    for n in list_4:
        i = 2
        while i <= n // i:
            if n % i == 0:
                s.add(i)
                while n % i == 0:
                    n //= i
            i += 1
        if n > 1:
            s.add(n)
    task_4_out = len(s)
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_1(val_1: int, y: int, bound: int) -> List[int]:
    ans = []
    a = 1
    while a <= bound:
        b = 1
        while a + b <= bound:
            ans.append(a + b)
            b *= y
            if y == 1:
                break
        if val_1 == 1:
            break
        a *= val_1
    task_1_out = list(ans)
    return task_1_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    ans = []
    (i, j) = (0, len(list_3) - 1)
    while i <= j:
        a = list_3[i] * list_3[i]
        b = list_3[j] * list_3[j]
        if a > b:
            ans.append(a)
            i += 1
        else:
            ans.append(b)
            j -= 1
    task_3_out = ans[::-1]
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    n = len(list_4)
    f = [0] * n
    g = [0] * n
    f[0] = int(list_4[0] > 0)
    g[0] = int(list_4[0] < 0)
    ans = f[0]
    for i in range(1, n):
        if list_4[i] > 0:
            f[i] = f[i - 1] + 1
            g[i] = 0 if g[i - 1] == 0 else g[i - 1] + 1
        elif list_4[i] < 0:
            f[i] = 0 if g[i - 1] == 0 else g[i - 1] + 1
            g[i] = f[i - 1] + 1
        ans = max(ans, f[i])
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    stk = []
    for x in list_1:
        if x > 0:
            stk.append(x)
        else:
            while stk and stk[-1] > 0 and (stk[-1] < -x):
                stk.pop()
            if stk and stk[-1] == -x:
                stk.pop()
            elif not stk or stk[-1] < 0:
                stk.append(x)
    task_1_out = stk
    return task_1_out
```

Let list_1 be the result of preprocessing task_1_input as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_1 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_1 and save the result in task_1_out.
```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    list_1.sort()
    n = len(list_1)
    f = [1] * n
    k = 0
    for i in range(n):
        for j in range(i):
            if list_1[i] % list_1[j] == 0:
                f[i] = max(f[i], f[j] + 1)
        if f[k] < f[i]:
            k = i
    m = f[k]
    i = k
    ans = []
    while m:
        if list_1[k] % list_1[i] == 0 and f[i] == m:
            ans.append(list_1[i])
            (k, m) = (i, m - 1)
        i -= 1
    task_1_out = ans
    return task_1_out
```

Task 2:
Let list_2 be the result of preprocessing task_1_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_2 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_2 with inputs limit = task_2_limit_static and save the result in task_2_out.
```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int], limit: int) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_2)
    arr = sorted(zip(list_2, range(n)))
    ans = [0] * n
    i = 0
    while i < n:
        j = i + 1
        while j < n and arr[j][0] - arr[j - 1][0] <= limit:
            j += 1
        idx = sorted((k for (_, k) in arr[i:j]))
        for (k, (x, _)) in zip(idx, arr[i:j]):
            ans[k] = x
        i = j
    task_2_out = ans
    return task_2_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_3 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_3 and save the result in task_3_out.
```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_3)
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    stk = []
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_3):
        while stk and list_3[stk[-1]] <= x:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_3[stk[-1]] <= list_3[i]:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    task_3_out = [r - l - 1 for (l, r) in zip(left, right)]
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int]) -> int:
    nums = [v - i for (i, v) in enumerate(list_4)]
    n = len(nums)
    left = [-1] * n
    stk = []
    for (i, v) in enumerate(nums):
        while stk and nums[stk[-1]] >= v:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    ans = 0
    dp = [0] * n
    dp[0] = list_4[0]
    for (i, v) in enumerate(list_4):
        j = left[i]
        cnt = min(v, i - j)
        u = v - cnt + 1
        s = (u + v) * cnt // 2
        dp[i] = s + (0 if j == -1 else dp[j])
        ans = max(ans, dp[i])
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    (i, j) = (0, len(list_2) - 1)
    while i < j:
        if list_2[i] % 2 == 0:
            i += 1
        elif list_2[j] % 2 == 1:
            j -= 1
        else:
            (list_2[i], list_2[j]) = (list_2[j], list_2[i])
```

```python
        if q not in s:
            ans.append(q)
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_3 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.

```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:

    def reverse(arr, j):
        i = 0
        while i < j:
            (arr[i], arr[j]) = (arr[j], arr[i])
            (i, j) = (i + 1, j - 1)
    n = len(list_3)
    ans = []
    for i in range(n - 1, 0, -1):
        j = i
        while j > 0 and list_3[j] != i + 1:
            j -= 1
        if j < i:
            if j > 0:
                ans.append(j + 1)
                reverse(list_3, j)
            ans.append(i + 1)
            reverse(list_3, i)
    task_3_out = ans
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 with inputs power = task_4_power_static and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int], power: int) -> int:
    list_4.sort()
    ans = score = 0
    (i, j) = (0, len(list_4) - 1)
    while i <= j:
        if power >= list_4[i]:
            power -= list_4[i]
            (score, i) = (score + 1, i + 1)
            ans = max(ans, score)
        elif score:
            power += list_4[j]
            (score, j) = (score - 1, j - 1)
        else:
            break
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int], arr2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    (i, j) = (len(list_4) - 1, len(arr2) - 1)
    c = 0
    ans = []
    while i >= 0 or j >= 0 or c:
        a = 0 if i < 0 else list_4[i]
        b = 0 if j < 0 else arr2[j]
        x = a + b + c
        c = 0
        if x >= 2:
            x -= 2
            c -= 1
        elif x == -1:
            x = 1
            c += 1
        ans.append(x)
        (i, j) = (i - 1, j - 1)
    while len(ans) > 1 and ans[-1] == 0:
        ans.pop()
    task_4_out = ans[::-1]
    return task_4_out
```

```python
    (i, j) = (0, len(list_1) - 1)
    while i < j:
        if list_1[i] % 2 == 0:
            i += 1
        elif list_1[j] % 2 == 1:
            j -= 1
```

Task 2:
Let list_2 be the result of preprocessing task_1_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_2)
    suf = [0] * (n + 1)
    s = set()
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        s.add(list_2[i])
        suf[i] = len(s)
    s.clear()
    ans = [0] * n
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_2):
        s.add(x)
        ans[i] = len(s) - suf[i + 1]
    task_2_out = ans
    return task_2_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_3 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_3 and save the result in task_3_out.
```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_3)
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    stk = []
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_3):
        while stk and list_3[stk[-1]] >= x:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_3[stk[-1]] >= list_3[i]:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    ans = [0] * n
    for i in range(n):
        m = right[i] - left[i] - 1
        ans[m - 1] = max(ans[m - 1], list_3[i])
    for i in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
        ans[i] = max(ans[i], ans[i + 1])
    task_3_out = ans
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_4 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_4 with inputs k = task_4_k_static and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int], k: int) -> int:
    list_4.sort()
    n = len(list_4)
    m = n >> 1
    ans = abs(list_4[m] - k)
    if list_4[m] > k:
        for i in range(m - 1, -1, -1):
            if list_4[i] <= k:
                break
            ans += list_4[i] - k
    else:
        for i in range(m + 1, n):
            if list_4[i] >= k:
                break
            ans += k - list_4[i]
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_1)
    left = [-1] * n
    right = [n] * n
    stk = []
    for (i, x) in enumerate(list_1):
        while stk and list_1[stk[-1]] <= x:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            left[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    stk = []
    for i in range(n - 1, -1, -1):
        while stk and list_1[stk[-1]] <= list_1[i]:
            stk.pop()
        if stk:
            right[i] = stk[-1]
        stk.append(i)
    task_1_out = [r - l - 1 for (l, r) in zip(left, right)]
    return task_1_out
```

Task 2:
Let list_2 be the result of preprocessing task_1_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_2 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_2 and save the result in task_2_out.
```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_2)
    leftSum = [0] * n
    for i in range(1, n):
        leftSum[i] = leftSum[i - 1] + list_2[i - 1]
    total = sum(list_2)
    answer = []
    for i in range(n):
        rightSum_i = total - list_2[i] - leftSum[i]
        answer.append(abs(leftSum[i] - rightSum_i))
    task_2_out = answer
    return task_2_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_3 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_3 and save the result in task_3_out.
```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> int:
    n = len(list_3)
    f = [0] * n
    g = [0] * n
    f[0] = int(list_3[0] > 0)
    g[0] = int(list_3[0] < 0)
    ans = f[0]
    for i in range(1, n):
        if list_3[i] > 0:
            f[i] = f[i - 1] + 1
            g[i] = 0 if g[i - 1] == 0 else g[i - 1] + 1
        elif list_3[i] < 0:
            f[i] = 0 if g[i - 1] == 0 else g[i - 1] + 1
            g[i] = f[i - 1] + 1
        ans = max(ans, f[i])
    task_3_out = ans
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let val_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
Trace the execution of task_4 and save the result in task_4_out.
```python
def task_4(val_4: int) -> int:
    while 1:
        (t, s, i) = (val_4, 0, 2)
        while i <= val_4 // i:
            while val_4 % i == 0:
                val_4 //= i
                s += i
            i += 1
        if val_4 > 1:
            s += val_4
        if s == t:
            task_4_out = t
            return task_4_out
        val_4 = s
```

Task 1:
Let list_1 be the result of preprocessing task_1_input as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_1 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_1 and save the result in task_1_out.
```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    f = True
    while f:
        f = False
        t = list_1[:]
        for i in range(1, len(t) - 1):
            if t[i] > t[i - 1] and t[i] > t[i + 1]:
                list_1[i] -= 1
                f = True
            if t[i] < t[i - 1] and t[i] < t[i + 1]:
                list_1[i] += 1
                f = True
    task_1_out = list_1
    return task_1_out
```

Task 2:
Let list_2 be the result of preprocessing task_1_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_2 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_2 with inputs limit = task_2_limit_static and save the result in task_2_out.
```python
def task_2(list_2: List[int], limit: int) -> List[int]:
    n = len(list_2)
    arr = sorted(zip(list_2, range(n)))
    ans = [0] * n
    i = 0
    while i < n:
        j = i + 1
        while j < n and arr[j][0] - arr[j - 1][0] <= limit:
            j += 1
        idx = sorted((k for (_, k) in arr[i:j]))
        for (k, (x, _)) in zip(idx, arr[i:j]):
            ans[k] = x
        i = j
    task_2_out = ans
    return task_2_out
```

Task 3:
Let list_3 be the result of preprocessing task_2_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.
If list_3 has more than 10 elements, keep only the first 10 elements.
Trace the execution of task_3 and save the result in task_3_out.
```python
def task_3(list_3: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    ans = []
    (i, j) = (0, len(list_3) - 1)
    while i <= j:
        a = list_3[i] * list_3[i]
        b = list_3[j] * list_3[j]
        if a > b:
            ans.append(a)
            i += 1
        else:
            ans.append(b)
            j -= 1
    task_3_out = ans[::-1]
    return task_3_out
```

Task 4:
Let list_4 be the result of preprocessing task_3_out as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

```python
def task_4(list_4: List[int], boardingCost: int, runningCost: int) -> int:
    ans = -1
    mx = t = 0
    wait = 0
    i = 0
    while wait or i < len(list_4):
        wait += list_4[i] if i < len(list_4) else 0
        up = wait if wait < 4 else 4
        wait -= up
        t += up * boardingCost - runningCost
        i += 1
        if t > mx:
            mx = t
            ans = i
    task_4_out = ans
    return task_4_out
```

Let list_1 be the result of preprocessing task_1_input as follows - for every element, if it is a float, convert it to an integer by rounding ties away from zero (0.5 to 1, -0.5 to -1); then replace it with the remainder of its absolute value modulo 100 while preserving its original sign.

Trace the execution of task_1 and save the result in task_1_out.
```python
def task_1(list_1: List[int]) -> List[int]:
    stk = []
    for x in list_1:
        if x > 0:
            stk.append(x)
        else:
            while stk and stk[-1] > 0 and (stk[-1] < -x):
                stk.pop()
            if stk and stk[-1] == -x:
                stk.pop()
            elif not stk or stk[-1] < 0:
                stk.append(x)
    task_1_out = stk
    return task_1_out
```
